########## NUMENOREAN ##########
################################
################################
				
### In order: 
# House of Elros - Kings of Numenor
# House of Elatan - Lords of Andúnië
# House of 	Vëantur - The Ship Captains of Numenor, later Princes of Dol Amroth
# House of Ciryamir - Family of the 5th Nazgul, Khôrahil
# House of Ruxöalëndil - Ancestors of the Ard the Silent
# House of Mornion, Founders of Korlea
# House of Ciryandur - Lords of Hazaj Tollin
# House of Borodiriath - Colonial overlords of Ûrêzâyan
# Herumor and Fuinur - Black Numenoreans that establish Kingdoms in Harad
# House of Ezirkhôn - Minor Numenorean family, lone survivor in Tûmag
# Family of Rendor, Lowborn Númenorean mariner and scholar

## Black Numenoreans of Umbar
# Colonial Sealords of Umbar - Various dynasties
# Lords of Dusalan - Various dynasties
# Lords of Zamadur and Annabrith - Various dynasties
# Lords of Caldur and Eradas - Various dynasties
# Lords of Sakal an-Khar - Various dynasties
# Lords of Barazon

###############################
##### The Kings of Numenor ####
###############################

			trait = lifestyle_mariner
			value = 85
		}
	}

	3911.1.1 = { #Downfall
		trait = depressed_1
		employer = lineborodiriath30
	}

	# Settles in Bellakar after Downfall, and despite his lack of a scholarly education, writes the important treatise 'The Missing Mountain'
	# In the book, he writes down his memories of the Three Prayers, and talks about the loss of the Meneltarma and the Line of Elros
	# At the time, Bellakar was struggling with this spiritually, as unlike the Westlands, they did not have Elendil and his new Mountain yet

	3916.7.7 = {
	    give_nickname = nick_of_nindamos #Nickname is given when he writes the book, as it references it
        effect = {
            add_character_flag = {
                flag = had_nickname_event
            }
        }
		trait = theologian
		trait = lifestyle_archivist
        add_trait_xp = {
			trait = lifestyle_archivist
			value = 15
		}
	}
	
	3917.9.16 = { #Dies, his book mostly finished. It becomes an important religious work in Bellakar
        death = { death_reason = death_laid_down_life }
    }
}

#### House of Beleth ##### 
## Descents of Beleth (lineofbeor22) of the House of Beor, family of Erendis Tar-Elestirne . Minor counts in Andunie in Numenor. ##

lineofbeleth1 = {				
	name = Beregar # Father of Erendis				
	dynasty = dynasty_beleth				
	religion = faith_numenorean				
	culture = numenorean				
			
	trait = education_diplomacy_2

	diplomacy = 8
	martial = 4
	stewardship = 7
	intrigue = 6
	learning = 9
	prowess = 10

	trait = ambitious
	trait = gregarious
	trait = compassionate

	trait = born_on_numenor
	trait = blood_of_numenor_10

	1300.9.21 = {				
		birth = yes			
		
	}
	1368.6.1 = { # 776 at age 68 
		add_spouse = lineofbeleth2
	}	
	1620.8.1 = { # 320 # Based on Tolkien's notes for Erendis's age in NM 320, rough = 90	
		death = { death_reason = death_laid_down_life } 			
	}				
}
